SUBENT        14027001   20250815                             152414027001    1 
BIB                 13         33                                 14027001    2 
TITLE      Measurements of (n,g) cross sections for very small    14027001    3 
           stable and radioactive samples of interest to the s-   14027001    4 
           and p-process                                          14027001    5 
AUTHOR     (P.E.Koehler,F.Kappeler)                               14027001    6 
REFERENCE  (C,94GATLIN,,179,1994)                                 14027001    7 
INSTITUTE  (1USALAS,2GERKFK)                                      14027001    8 
FACILITY   (LINAC,1USALAS) The Los Alamos Neutron Scattering      14027001    9 
           Center (LANSCE).                                       14027001   10 
INC-SOURCE Spallation from proton + W.                            14027001   11 
DETECTOR   (SCIN) A pair of deuterated benzene C6D6 scintillators.14027001   12 
SAMPLE     Both the 191,193Ir samples were highly enriched.       14027001   13 
           191Ir and 193Ir were measured using 1 mg and 2 mg      14027001   14 
           samples, respectively. The samples consisted of        14027001   15 
           metallic powder which had been "super-glued" to 0.8    14027001   16 
           microm-thick aluminum backing foils.                   14027001   17 
METHOD     The gamma-ray yield as a function of energy was        14027001   18 
           measured down to thermal energy and the measured       14027001   19 
           thermal cross sections were used to normalize the      14027001   20 
           yields to absolute cross sections. The total beam      14027001   21 
           time was about 1 day for each sample. The experiment   14027001   22 
           was performed on flight path 4 at LANSCE to            14027001   23 
           demonstrate the feasibility of measurements on very    14027001   24 
           small samples.                                         14027001   25 
ERR-ANALYS (DATA-ERR) The uncertainties are 1-sigma in barns.     14027001   26 
CORRECTION The data have not been corrected for self shielding    14027001   27 
           and multiple scattering. The 191Ir data have been      14027001   28 
           corrected for the small amount of 193Ir in the         14027001   29 
           enriched 191Ir sample and vice versa.                  14027001   30 
STATUS     (APRVD) Approved by P.E.Koehler on August 21, 2025.    14027001   31 
HISTORY    (20050710C) DR                                         14027001   32 
           (20250815A) BP: Updated INSTITUTE and SAMPLE, added    14027001   33 
           METHOD, ERR-ANALYS, CORRECTION, replaced digitized     14027001   34 
           data with the original.                                14027001   35
